inspections at least 48 hours before commencing any work in conjunction with the stormwater management plan and upon completion of the project when a final inspection will be conducted b the developer shall retain a professional engineer licensed in the state to conduct inspections written inspection reports shall be made of the periodic inspections necessary during construction of stormwater management systems to ensure compliance with the approved plans c written inspection reports shall be provided to the developer and the iwc and shall include 1 the date and location of the inspection  2 whether construction was in compliance with the approved stormwater management plan  3 any variations from the approved construction specifications  and 4 any violations that exist d the ownerdeveloper and onsite personnel shall be notified in writing when violations are observed written notification shall describe the nature of the violation and the required corrective action e no work shall proceed until the iwc its agents or the town engineer approves the work previously completed the inspector shall provide the developer and the iwc with the results of the inspection reports as soon as possible after completion of each required inspection 1  81 inspection requirements during construction a at a minimum inspections shall be made and documented at the following specified stages of construction 1 for ponds a upon completion of excavation to subfoundation and when required installation of structural supports or reinforcement for structures including but not limited to i core trenches for structural embankments  ii inlet and outlet structures antiseep collars or diaphragms and watertight connectors on pipes  and iii trenches for enclosed storm drainage facilities b during placement of structural fill concrete and installation of piping and catch basins  c during backfill of foundations and trenches  d during embankment construction  and e upon completion of final grading and establishment of permanent stabilization 2 wetlandsat the stages specified for pond construction in subsection 4252a1 during and after wetland reservoir area planting and during the second growing season to verify a vegetation survival rate of at least 50 percent 3 for infiltration trenches a during excavation to subgrade  b during placement and backfill of underdrain systems and observation wells  c during placement of geotextiles and all filter media  d during construction of appurtenant conveyance systems such as diversion structures prefilters and filters inlets outlets and flow distribution structures  and e upon completion of final grading and establishment of permanent stabilization  4 for infiltration basinsat the stages specified for pond construction in subsection 4252a1 and during placement and backfill of underdrain systems 5 for filtering systems a during excavation to subgrade  b during placement and backfill of underdrain systems  c during placement of geotextiles and all filter media  d during construction of appurtenant conveyance systems such as flow diversion structures prefilters and filters inlets outlets orifices and flow distribution structures  and e upon completion of final grading and establishment of permanent stabilization 6 for open channel systems a during excavation to subgrade  b during placement and backfill of underdrain systems for dry swales  c during installation of diaphragms check dams or weirs  and d upon completion of final grading and establishment of permanent stabilization 7 for nonstructural practicesupon completion of final grading the establishment of permanent stabilization and before issuance of use and occupancy approval b the iwc may for enforcement purposes use any one or a combination of the following actions 1 a notice of violation shall be issued specifying the need for a violation to be corrected if the stormwater management plan noncompliance is identified  2 a stop work order shall be issued for the site by the iwc its agents or the town engineer if a violation persists  3 bonds or securities may be withheld or the case may be referred for legal action if reasonable efforts to correct the violation have not been undertaken  or 4 in addition to any other sanctions a civil action or criminal prosecution may be brought against any person in violation this article c any step in the enforcement process may be taken at any time depending on the severity of the violation d once construction is complete asbuilt plan certification shall be submitted by a professional engineer licensed in the state to ensure that constructed stormwater management practices and conveyance systems comply with the specifications contained in the approved plans at a minimum asbuilt certification shall include a set of drawings comparing the approved stormwater management plan with what was constructed the iwc may require additional information 1  82 secs 42534260  reserved division 8  maintenance maintenance inspection a the iwc shall ensure that all stormwater management systems are inspected for performance of preventative maintenance inspection shall occur during the first year of operation and at least once every three 3 years thereafter in addition a maintenance agreement between the owner and the iwc shall be executed for privately owned stormwater management systems as described in section 4262 b the iwc shall maintain inspection reports for all stormwater management systems c inspection reports for stormwater management systems shall include the following 1 the date of inspection  2 name of inspector  3 the condition of a vegetation or filter media  b fences or other safety devices  c spillways valves or other control structures  d embankments slopes and safety benches  e reservoir or treatment areas  f inlet and outlet channels or structures  g underground drainage  h sediment and debris accumulation in storage and forebay areas  i any nonstructural practices to the extent practicable  and j any other item that could affect the proper function of the stormwater management system 4 description of needed maintenance d after notification is provided to the owner of any deficiencies discovered from an inspection of a stormwater management system the owner shall have 30 days or other time frame mutually agreed to between the iwc and the owner to correct the deficiencies the iwc shall then conduct a subsequent inspection to ensure completion of the repairs e if repairs are not undertaken or are not done properly then enforcement procedures of subsection 4262c shall be followed by the iwc f if after an inspection by the iwc the condition of a stormwater management facility presents an immediate danger to the public health or safety because of an unsafe condition or improper maintenance the iwc shall take such action as may be necessary to protect the public and make the facility safe any cost incurred by the town of seymour shall be assessed against the owners as provided in subsection 4262c 1  91 maintenance agreement a prior to the issuance of any building permit for which stormwater management is required the iwc shall require the applicant or owner to execute an inspection and maintenance agreement binding on all subsequent owners of land served by a private stormwater management facility such agreement shall provide for access to the facility at reasonable times for regular inspections by the iwc or its authorized representative to ensure that the facility is maintained in proper working condition to meet design standards b the applicant andor owner shall record the agreement in the land records of the town c the agreement shall also provide that if after notice by the iwc its agents or the town engineer to correct a violation requiring maintenance work satisfactory corrections are not made by the owners within a reasonable period of time 30 days maximum the iwc may perform all necessary work to place the facility in proper working condition the owners of the facility shall be assessed the cost of the work and any penalties this may be accomplished by placing a lien on the property which may be placed on the tax bill and collected as ordinary taxes by the town 1  92 maintenance responsibility a the owner of the property on which work has been done pursuant to this ordinance for private stormwater management facilities or any other person or agent in control of such property shall maintain in good condition and promptly repair and restore all grade surfaces walls drains dams and structures vegetation erosion and sediment control measures and other protective devices such repairs or restoration and maintenance shall be in accordance with approved plans b a maintenance schedule shall be developed for the life of any stormwater management facility and shall state the maintenance to be completed the time period for completion and who shall perform the maintenance this maintenance schedule shall be printed on the approved stormwater management plan 1  93 civil service footnotes  1  editors note the civil service have been largely provided by the editor charter reference board of library directors  51  civil service commissioner  103  town employees  111 et seq cross reference administration  21 et seq  building inspector  426 et seq  fire department  621 et seq  housing code enforcement officer  961 et seq  library  1216 et seq  sewer inspector  1786 et seq article i  purpose civil service established there is hereby established a civil service system for the town of seymour the civil service commission shall have such duties and responsibilities as are granted to it by charter in section 103 and sections 111113 of said charter  101 purpose it shall be the purpose of the civil service system to provide the means for selecting andor promoting employees in the classified service solely on the basis of proven ability to perform the duties required as set forth by the specific job descriptions set forth in this ordinance it is hereby declared the personnel policy of the town of seymour that employment by the town in the classified service shall be based solely on merit and fitness free of personal and political considerations appointments shall be based on systematic tests and evaluation it is the desire of the town that high morals shall be maintained by the fair administration of the merit system established under this ordinance  102 secs 4534520  reserved article ii  definitions definitions of words and terms used in this chapter the following words terms and phrases when used in this chapter shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this section except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning appointing authority the board of selectmen has the power and shall be the appointing authority for all civil service positions with the exception of the position of head librarian with relation to the head librarian the appointing authority shall be the library board of directors civil service positions the classified service positions shall be full time nonunion employees of the town of seymour the following will not be included within the classified service a elective officials and persons appointed to fill vacancies in elective offices b members of boards and other officers who are administrative appointments of the first selectman and the board of selectman unless otherwise provided by charter c employees of the board of education d persons employed for a temporary or part time position eligibility list the eligibility list shall consist of those who have completed all elements of the testing procedure established by this ordinance said list shall include the applicants name final grade and rank this list shall remain in effect for a period of one year eligible person for positions the candidates who rank the highest as recommended by the civil service commission shall be eligible for consideration and appointment to the position to be filled the civil service commission shall present a list of such persons to the appointing authority for interview and appointment full time employee a full time employee shall be an employee who is employed in a civil service position as a permanent full time employee for 30 or more hours weekly any person who is permanently employed in one or more positions for a cumulative time of 30 hours or more hours will be considered fulltime any person holding a full time position in the municipal government as of  shall be retained without preliminary or performance tests and shall thereafter be subject to all other respects to the provisions of this chapter permanent employee a permanent employee shall be an employee who successfully completes the probationary period and has been permanently appointed as provided in these policies and procedures  201207 secs 45214530  reserved article iii  grievance procedure applicability the following procedure applies to members of the classified service who have completed the probationary period  30 purpose the purpose of the grievance procedure shall be to settle employees grievances on as low an administrative level as possible and practical so as to insure efficiency and employee morale  31 grievance defined a grievance is defined as a dispute between an employee andor the department head and the town over the interpretation or application of a specific section in the civil service ordinance town charter or regulations  32 filing of grievances grievances must be filed in writing within 14 calendar days of the incident giving rise to the grievance all grievances shall be administered in accordance with the procedure set forth below  33 representation by counsel an employee may be represented by counsel at each and every step of the grievance procedure the employee shall bear the sole cost of the employment of said counsel  34 working day defined for purposes of grievance procedure for the purpose of the grievance procedure a working day is defined as monday including holidays  35 grievance procedurestep 1 an employee or his or her legal counsel if represented may submit a written grievance in accordance with this section to the first selectman or in his absence to his designee and the appropriate department head the first selectman or said designee and the appropriate department head will make an effort to resolve the grievance and will render an answer in writing to the grievance within ten working days of receipt of the grievance this answer will be provided to the aggrieved employee and to his counsel if represented in the case of the head librarian the grievance will be submitted to the library board of directors  36 samestep 2 if the aggrieved employee and the counsel is not satisfied with the decision rendered by the first selectman or his designee and the said department head they may submit the grievance in writing to the full board of selectmen within seven working days of the decision the full board of selectmen shall consider the grievance at its next scheduled meeting which shall not be more than 15 days after the receipt of the grievance by the board of selectmen and shall render an answer to the grievance within seven working days after such scheduled meeting to the aggrieved employee and his counsel if represented in the case of the head librarian the second step of the grievance procedure shall be to the library board of directors  37 samestep 3 if the aggrieved employee and his legal counsel if represented are not satisfied with the decision rendered by the board of selectmen or library board of directors they may appeal in writing to the full civil service commission not later than ten calendar days after receipt of the decision of the board of selectmen or library board of directors the full civil service commission shall schedule a hearing with the aggrieved employee and his legal counsel if represented at the next scheduled meeting after receipt of the appeal the full civil service commission will decide only one grievance per session the full civil service commission shall make the final decision on the grievance after a full hearing such decision will be in writing and shall be made within ten working days of the hearing the full civil service commission will hear both sides involved in the grievance  38 secs 45404550  reserved article iv  classification classification plan a the following constitute the positions to be included within the classification plan of the civil service system 1 finance director  2 foreman of public works  3 head librarian  4 superintendentwaste water control b the duties responsibilities and minimum qualifications of the aforesaid civil service positions shall be as set forth in this section  41 42  2 secs 45524560  reserved article v  compensation salary schedule to be established for each classified position the town shall establish a schedule which shall contain a minimum salary and a maximum salary  51 consideration for pay increases at the recommendation of the first selectman with the approval of the majority of the board of selectmen employees in civil service will be considered for pay increases once per year the board of selectmen will make these recommendations to the board of finance by february 15 to be effective july 1 of the same year in the case of the head librarian any such recommendations shall be made by the library board of directors  52 satisfactory service required for salary increase increase in salary for individual employees shall be primarily based upon satisfactory service  53 minimum rate of pay the minimum rate of pay for a particular position shall normally be offered for recruitment purposes the first selectman may with the approval of the board of selectmen offer a rate of pay above the minimum provided however that the qualifications of the applicant are superior to those of competing applicants andor employees cannot be secured at the minimum rate due to a shortage of qualified applicants available at the minimum rate  54 compensation upon reassignment if a town employee is temporarily reassigned to a position of higher level pay compensation will be based upon the higher salary for the duration of the reassignment reassignment must be for a period of at least 30 days to receive a higher salary if reassigned at a lower level of pay compensation will be based upon employees present salary  55 compensation for probational employees the compensation for probational employees will be set forth for each position in the compensation schedule established in section 4561 such compensation will not be adjusted except with the majority approval of the board of selectmen probationary employees will not receive entry level salary until the probationary period has been completed  56 vacation leave permanent full time employees under civil service will be entitled to the following vacation time two weeks after 12 months employment three weeks after five years employment one extra day for each additional year of employment after ten years with a maximum of four weeks after 15 years of continuous employment after 20 years of continuous employment the maximum vacation will be five weeks any vacation leave shall be taken within the fiscal year in which it was earned any existing contract dealing with affected employees will be honored  57 paid holidays the following holidays shall be observed by all permanent full time employees and shall be granted with pay new years day martin luther king day presidents day good friday memorial day independence day labor day columbus day veterans day election day thanksgiving day day after thanksgiving christmas eve day christmas the half day on december 31 when a holiday falls on a saturday the day before the holiday will be observed when the holiday fails on a sunday the day after the holiday will be observed there will however be no compensation day given if christmas eve day or december 31 falls on a saturday or sunday in the case of the head librarian at the discretion of the library board of directors the library may remain open on the following holidays martin luther king day presidents day columbus day election day and the day after thanksgiving if the library is opened on such days the head librarian shall be entitled to such floating holiday in compensation said floating holiday shall be taken within two weeks of the holiday upon which the library remains open in the case of the foreman of the department of public works such employee shall be entitled to the same holidays as granted under the contract provided for the union members of the department of public works  58 sick leave all permanent full time employees shall be granted sick leave with pay at the rate of one and onequarter 114 days per month 15 sick days per year are the maximum allowed after five consecutive sick days are used under this section a doctors slip must be presented before an employee may be permitted to return to work  59 accumulation of unused sick leave a no unused sick leave of any employee may be accumulated after  employees may retain the unused sick leave accumulated prior to  but no further accumulations earned after that date will be permitted unused sick leave accumulated prior to  may be used in one of the following ways 1 the employee may use sick accumulation as sick leave 2 the employee may use such accumulation until termination of his employment as vacation time subject to the approval of the board of selectmen or of the library board of directors subject to departmental needs 3 the employee may elect to retain such accumulation until termination of his employment at which time the employee shall be paid at 50 percent of his prevailing day rate as of  times the number of days accumulated b as of  in the final pay period of each fiscal year each employee shall be paid 66 23 percent the value of each sick day remaining unused for that year should an employee be paid for a day subsequently used the day shall be deducted from the employees next pay check  510 leave of absence without pay the first selectman with the majority vote of the board of selectmen or the library board of directors in the case of the head librarian may grant leave of absence without pay to any employee upon the employees request such leave shall be for a period not to exceed three months this leave of absence must be due to illness or personal problems no employee will be granted a leave of absence to work at another job  511 paid personal leave each full time employee will be allowed three personal days off each year if these are not used no compensation will be given  512 group insurance group insurance will be granted to all civil service employees and retirees who retire after the age 5912 at the towns expense in accordance with the towns group insurance plan or such plan as the town may adopt in the future such insurance benefits may be offered to said employees families at the employees expense  513 retirement benefits retirement benefits will be granted in accordance with the municipal retirement plan  514 funeral leave all full time civil service employees will be allowed funeral leave as follows 1 three days for spouses children parents parentsinlaw brother and sister 2 one day for other relatives who shall include uncle aunt cousin brotherinlaw sisterinlaw permission to attend the funeral service of a close acquaintance without compensation may be obtained from the first selectman or in the case of the head librarian from the library board of directors  515 leave for jury duty employees shall be granted leaves of absence for required jury duty such employees shall receive the portion of their regular salary which will together with their pay for jury duty or fees equal their total salary for the same period pay vouchers shall be submitted to ascertain the pay due to the employee  516 military training duty leave military training duty leave shall be granted to regular employees when they are required to serve on active reserve or on national guard duty such employees shall receive that portion of their regular salary which will with their pay for military service equal their total salary for the same period  517 compensation for use of private automobile for official town business an employee authorized by the immediate supervisor to use his private automobile for official town business shall be compensated at a rate established by the board of selectmen claims must be submitted weekly to the supervisor vehicles must be properly insured indemnifying the town against liability  518 accumulated vacation leave and extra hours worked upon adoption of this ordinance all accumulated vacations and extra hours worked which have been approved by the department head will be honored all new vacation days and extra time must adhere to the above provisions  519 secs 45804590  reserved article vi  recruitment announcement of vacancies a the first selectman or the library board of directors with regard to the position of head librarian shall make known all permanent vacancies for all positions in civil service to the civil service commission within ten days of notification of vacancies the civil service commission will post announcements for such vacancies in at least one newspaper having general circulation in the area and in such other places they deem necessary at the time such permanent vacancies are given to said commission in writing from the first selectman or the library board of directors all persons on the eligibility list or employees who wish to transfer will be considered b any announcement for vacancies shall include the following 1 job title  2 salary ranges  3 nature of work  4 minimum qualifications  5 closing date for application and 6 any additional information regarding the position deemed necessary by the civil service commission  60 61 application for employment application shall be made on forms provided by the first selectman library board of directors all applications will be available at the first selectmans office or the library board of directors and when completed will be returned there when all applications have been returned and the closing date has passed the first selectman or the library board of directors will turn the applications over to the civil service commission for review  62 security of personal information as part of the application procedure references provided by the applicants shall be reviewed by the civil service commission all such information is to be treated as privileged information all such personal information will be secured in locked files andor compartments in the first selectmans office the board of selectmen andor the library board of directors will determine who has access to the files  63 grounds for rejection of application the civil service commission shall be authorized to reject any application for the following reasons 1 lack of education experience andor qualifications 2 conviction of a felony infamous crime or crime involving moral turpitude 3 falsifying any part of the application 4 use of political pressure or bribery to secure the position 5 direct or indirect knowledge of the contents of any part of the examination to which the applicant was not entitled 6 involvement in the completion administration or correction of the examination 7 failure to submit completed examination within the allotted time  64 notification of rejections whenever an application is rejected the civil service commission shall notify the applicant in writing certified mail return receipt requested of such rejection the letter shall include a notice informing the applicant of his right to review pursuant to section 4596 hereof  65 right of review any applicant whose application has been rejected may request in writing a review of said application such request shall be made prior to any examination for the position in question the decision of the civil service commission shall be final the civil service commission shall have the power to allow the applicant to take part in the examination pending their review of the appeal  66 policy of nondiscrimination no person applying for a position with the town of seymour shall be discriminated against because of race religion sex age national origin or political affiliation  67 secs 459845110  reserved article vii  examinations examination may be required all appointments to positions within the civil service of the town of seymour shall be made as provided herein the examination and testing for each position shall be set forth in each job description where examinations are required  70 examination process the impartial examination process shall be of a practical nature and shall relate to subjects which in the opinion of the civil service commission fairly measure the relative capabilities of persons examined to execute the duties and responsibilities of the position sought for positions involving semiskilled or unskilled labor or custodial work the civil service system may adopt or authorize use of other procedures as they determine may be appropriate while assuring a selection of such employees on the basis of merit and fitness unless otherwise provided by the job description  71 types of examination except as otherwise provided by ordinance the type of examination shall be determined by the civil service commission and may include but shall not be limited to written oral physical mental andor performance or any combination thereof the department head shall be consulted as to the type of examination given in each instance  72 examinations to be openly competitive all examinations shall be of an open competitive nature and all applicants meeting the prescribed requirements shall be allowed to participate except as noted in section 45117 of this chapter  73 use of outside testing agencies the civil service commission shall be allowed to contract with any competent agency or individual for the purpose of preparing and for administering such examinations in the absence of such contract the civil service commission or a portion thereof shall perform said duties or may delegate their performance  74 notification of applicants all qualified applicants shall be notified in writing of the time place and date of the examination by the civil service commission  75 applicant required to pass each part of examination in any examination process which requires more than one test the applicant shall be required to achieve the passing grade for each test in order to continue the examination process if the applicant fails to achieve the passing grade in any part of the examination process then he will not be allowed to continue and shall be notified in writing by the civil service commission if the applicant in such an examination achieves a passing grade in any part of the examination process than he shall be allowed to continue and shall be notified in writing by the civil service commission of his grade and the date of the next part of the examination process  76 promotional examinations promotional examinations within the civil service system shall be of a competitive nature and shall in general be as provided in sections 45112 and 45113 with due allowance for difference due to the promotional nature of the examination  77 right of employees to apply for examinations no department head or administrator shall deny any employee permission to apply for any examination  78 notification of final grade each applicant who has completed all phases of the examination procedure shall be notified in writing by the civil service commission of his final grade rank  79 right to inspect examination papers each applicant shall be entitled to inspect his examination papers andor grading papers under conditions prescribed by the civil service commission  710 passing grade to be announced in advance the passing grade for each examination or part thereof shall be determined and announced in advance by the civil service commission  711 secs 4512345130  reserved article viii  appointments eligibility list prepared the civil service commission shall prepare an eligibility list of all applicants who have successfully completed the testing procedure said eligibility list shall include the applicants name final grade and rank this list shall remain in effect for a period of one year and may be extended by the civil service commission for an additional one year  80 annual update of eligibility list the civil service commission or its designee shall onor before the anniversary date of the eligibility list contact those persons whose names appear on said list to inquire whether or not they wish to have their names remain on said list those applicants who desire their names to be removed shall notify the civil service commission in writing and said notice shall be attached to the eligibility list  81 use of eligibility list in filling vacancy when a vacancy is to be filled the civil service commission shall certify to the appointing authority the names of the top three persons from the eligibility list a recommendation to the appointing authority shall also be made from the applicable department head  82 appointing authority to approve eligible applicant the appointing authority ie the board of selectmen or library board of directors shall select an applicant from said certified list said selection shall be by majority vote of the board of selectmen or library board of directors where a quorum is present the applicant chosen shall be notified in writing by certified mail of such appointment and shall accept said appointment within seven days one representative of the civil service commission and the appropriate department head shall have the right to be present when the appointing authority considers the appointment  83 failure of applicant to accept position if the applicant fails to accept within the allowed time period then the appointing authority shall select another applicant from the certified list this procedure shall be continued until a successful candidate accepts the position or until the certified list is exhausted  84 provisional appointment without examination provisional appointments without examination may be made only when there is no certified list for no more than six months and except as provided in section 45137 only of persons qualified  85 emergency appointment in the event of an emergency the appointing authority may appoint any individual to a position to prevent the stoppage of public business andor loss or serious inconvenience to the public for a period not greater that 60 days such appointment shall be valid only for the duration of said emergency but in any event not longer than 60 days  86 secs 4513845150  reserved article ix  probation probationary period required for new employees all new employees shall be required to serve a probationary period of six months  90 performance reports during the probationary period of any new employee the supervisor in charge of the department shall submit to the appointing authority a written performance report at the end of 30 days 90 days and three weeks prior to the end of the employees probationary period such reports and their approval by the appointing authority are definite requisites for permanent appointment and the privileges that accompany it  91 termination after thirty working days an employee may be terminated at any time after 30 working days of probationary period by the appointing authority on the written recommendation of the department head that the employee failed to meet the minimum standards for the performance of the job  92 notice of unsatisfactory performance or deficiencies within two months from the beginning of a probationary period the department head shall in writing notice the employee if he she is not performing satisfactorily the notice shall detail the areas of the job in which the department head feels the employee is not performing to standard  93 no appeal of termination during probationary period there shall be no appeal of the decision to terminate a probationary employee  94 successful completion of probationary period upon successful completion of the stated probationary period the first selectman shall notify the employee of his permanent status with the town of seymour in the case of the head librarian the responsible for all employees in their departments any problems concerning an employee will be reported by the department head to the first selectmen who will report same to the board of selectmen where appropriate action will be taken in the case of the head librarian any problems concerning same will be reported to the library board of directors where appropriate action will be taken b time to time by said town  111 participation in connecticut municipal retirement system said employees shall also be subject to the towns participation in the connecticut municipal retirement system  112 secs 4519345200  reserved article xii  disciplinary procedures reasons for disciplinary action disciplinary action against any employee shall be taken only for one or more but not limited to the following reasons 1 dishonesty defined as including falsification of records financial dishonesty fraud theft and willful misrepresentation  2 insubordination defined as refusal to carry out orders of the department head or first selectman or of any person delegated authority over the employee  3 action detrimental to the town defined as the use of alcohol drugs or excess of temperament which impede the conduct of daily business  4 violence threats of violence or insults defined as assaults upon fellow workers or on any person who is transacting business verbal abuse which includes but is not limited to abusive language directed at any of the foregoing or participation in any action which endanger the bodily safety of any of the foregoing  5 criminal conduct defined as a conviction of a misdemeanor involving the theft of property or misappropriation of funds or of any felony committed while in the employ of the town or theft or destruction of town property  6 deficiency in performance of work defined as inefficiency habitual tardiness or absenteeism the performance of unauthorized services for others during work hours  the refusal or failure to perform a designated quantity and quality of work  or fraudulently obtaining sick or injury leave 7 unauthorized political activity defined as engaging in political activity prohibited by section 112 of the town charter  and 8 any other conduct materially impairing the efficiently with which the town government provides services to the citizens of the community  121 classes of disciplinary action there shall be three classes of disciplinary action these classes progress from class i to class iii depending on the repetition andor severity of the offense class i disciplinary action can be taken at the discretion of the individual department head any action taken in class ii may be taken with the approval of the first selectman class iii disciplinary action may only be taken with the approval of the majority of the board of selectmen with regard to the head librarian all disciplinary action may only be taken with the approval of the majority of the library board of directors and the references to the department head and first selectman shall be intended to refer to the library board of directors concerning the head librarian  122 disciplinary actionclass i class i disciplinary action consists of a written reprimand after oral discussions with the employee and the department head a copy of said reprimand is sent to the first selectman to be placed in the employees permanent file the employee upon receipt of said reprimand may request a hearing with the first selectman to discuss the nature of the disciplinary action the first selectman may upon hearing the employees and department head statements decide whether or not to place the written reprimand in the employees permanent file  123 sameclass ii a a class ii disciplinary action shall consist of suspension without pay this may be imposed after a series of repeated offenses or after a serious offense the employee must be notified at least three days before the effective date of any such action this letter of notification must clearly state the nature of the offense the length of the suspension and the fact that the employee may appeal the ordered absence without pay a maximum penalty under class ii action shall be a suspension to a maximum of five working days b within the threeday notification period the individual may request an appointment with the first selectman who on the basis of the employees and department heads statements andor results of an investigation may determine whether of not the suspension will remain in effect the letter of notification to the employee must bear the signatures of both the department head and the first selectman  124 125 sameclass iii a there are two sections to a class iii disciplinary action and they are as follows 1 demotion the transfer of an employee to a lower grade and 2 dismissal the complete separation of an employee from employment with the town b the procedure for both sections of class iii are the same any action taken in this class must be approved by the board of selectmen except in the case of the head librarian which shall require the approval of a majority of the board of library directors the signature of the first selectman and the department head or the president of the library board of directors must appear on the letter of notification which is sent to the individual and the civil service commission by certified mail c the letter of notification must clearly state the nature of the offense advise the employee of his right to appeal to the civil service commission and state that the appeal must be taken within 14 days of the effective date of action  126 127 secs 4520645210  reserved article xiii  separations separations generally a the tenure of every employee shall be conditioned upon behavior satisfactory performance of duties satisfactory attendance and continued capability for the job position b resignation layoff dismissal disability death and retirement are considered separations all separations shall be accomplished in the manner indicated at the time of separation and prior to final payment to the employee all records assets or other items of town property in the employees custody shall be transferred to the department head or in the case of a department head to the first selectman in the case of the head librarian such transfer shall be made to the library board of directors any amount due because of shortage in the above accounting shall be withheld from the employees final compensation or collected appropriate action  130 131 payment for earned salary and vacation leave employees who leave the town service in good standing shall receive payment for all earned salary and vacation leave subject to deductions made pursuant to section 131b effective  such payments shall include sick leave earned  132 reasons for separation employees may be separated from employment with the town for the following reasons 1 disciplinary termination as set forth in 2 medical termination upon certification by a physician that the individual is not physically or in the alternative mentally capable of carrying out the duties of his position if there is a disagreement between the employee and the town as to the existence of such disability the employee shall have the right of appeal to the civil service commission 3 resignation any employee in good standing desiring to leave the position shall submit a written resignation stating the effective date such notice should be at lest 14 days prior to the desired date of termination the department head may permit a shorter period of notice because of unusual circumstances the resignation shall be forwarded to the first selectman with a statement by the department head as to the resigned employees service performance in case of the head librarian such notice shall be forwarded to the library board of directors a copy of such notice shall be placed in the personnel file of the employee 4 reduction of force a when a position must be discontinued or abolished because of lack of work or lack of funds the department head andor the first selectman may recommend that such action of discontinuance be taken the first selectman with the concurrence of a majority of the board of selectmen may discontinue such positions because of lack of work or funds in the case of the head librarian the library board of directors may take such action by a majority vote of the board b the first selectman by virtue of a majority vote of the board of selectmen shall determine the order of layoff of employees on basis of the relative suitability for the jobs that remain and the length of continuous service with the town if it is found that two or more persons in a department in which a layoff is to be made have equal ratings the order of layoff in such cases shall be in the inverse order of the date of initial employment in the case of the head librarian the library board of directors shall have the power to determine the order of layoff c in normal circumstances permanent employees subject to layoff shall be notified in writing two calendar weeks prior to the effective date d any laidoff employee shall have the right to be recalled if the position again becomes open notice of recall shall be given in writing by certified mail return receipt requested and must be accepted in writing within ten days of receipt if the employee elects not to return to work his employment with the town shall be automatically terminated 5 failure to meet performance standards during first 30 days of probationary period at any time subsequent to the first 30 days during the probationary period the first selectman upon the recommendation of the department head may separate an employee whose performance does not meet required standards with the concurrence of a majority vote of the board of selectmen in the case of the head librarian such action may be taken with the concurrence of a majority vote of the library board of directors 6 death separation shall be effective as of the date of death all compensation due shall be paid to the estate of the employee except for such sums as by law may be due to the surviving spouse  133 secs 4521445220  reserved article xiv  records first selectman the first selectman shall maintain adequate records of the proceedings of the board of selectman and of his own official acts  141 civil service commission the civil service commission shall maintain an adequate record of the examination record of every candidate and the employment record of every employee said records shall general fire zones a definition a fire zone is a designated unobstructed passageway sufficient in size to permit free passage of fire and other emergency equipment from a public highway to all necessary areas or portions of any private or public property as hereinafter set forth b establishment by fire marshal whenever the fire marshal shall determine that the reasonable safety of persons occupying or using any premises public or private having a capacity of at least 15 persons requires the establishment of a fire zone for orderly access of fire and other emergency equipment for the protection of public safety he shall establish such fire zone by written order and cause to be made public announcement of such fire zone establishment by posting the same on the town post in town hall he shall cause a copy of such order to be delivered to the owner or owners or agents thereof of any private land on which such fire zone is established c order establishing fire zone  appeal to board of selectmen whenever the fire marshal establishes a fire zone he shall file one copy of his order with the town clerk and one copy with the board of police commissioners any person aggrieved by such order may file with the town clerk within 15 days after the date of such order written notice of appeal setting forth therein reasons of aggrievement a copy of the appeal shall be transmitted forth with by the town clerk to the board of selectmen after hearing the board of selectmen may affirm modify or rescind such order d signs delineating fire zone  cost  lien upon establishment of a fire zone the board of police commissioners shall cause to be erected or installed adequate signs markings and other devices to delineate the fire zone signs markings and other devices erected or installed on privately owned premises shall be the cost of the private owner and may be billed for and collected in the same manner as municipal taxes provided the board of police commissioners causes a notice of lien to be filed on the land records within 60 days after such erection or installation e parking etc in fire zone  fine for violations no person shall park or permit to stand a motor vehicle in a fire zone which has been established in accordance with this section except when actually picking up or discharging passengers any person violating this section shall be fined not more than $2500 the registered owner of a motor vehicle shall be presumed to be the operator of such vehicle f notice of violation  appearance at police department and payment prior to time specified in notice whenever a vehicle is found standing in violation of subsection e a police officer shall serve upon the owner or operator of such vehicle or place upon such vehicle a notice directing the owner or operator thereof to appear at the police department prior to a time specified in the notice if any person receiving the notice shall appear as directed and shall pay an amount as specified in the notice not exceeding $200 such payment shall bar a prosecution for violation of subsection e  unauthorized removal use of equipment  use outside town a if any person shall take or remove any of the ladders or implements for extinguishing fires belonging to the town from the place where deposited except in case of fire or inspection or shall use any such ladders or other implements or cause the same to be used when so taken such person shall pay a fine of $500 b no fire apparatus belonging to the town shall be taken outside the town without the express permission of the chief or his assistants  fire marshals office inspection and permit fees the fire marshal shall submit to the board of selectmen a schedule of recommended fire inspection permit and document fees when requested by department provide for its government gs 7301  provisions concerning volunteer departments gs  73147323 division 1  generally officers members the fire department shall consist of a fire chief one or more assistant chiefs and duly enlisted volunteers the chief and assistant chiefs shall be appointed annually prior to the last week in june by the board of fire commissioners and shall hold office for one year from july 1 or until others are appointed in their stead or until they are disabled and incapacitated for such office the board of fire commissioners shall fill any vacancy that may occur in the office of chief or assistant chiefs within a reasonable time of the occurrence thereof the chief and assistant chiefs may be removed for cause by the board of fire commissioners after a full hearing the chief and assistant chiefs shall be residents of the town of seymour   1 eff 12709  1 enlistment qualifications of volunteers the department shall consist of not more than 200 people and shall be filled by voluntary enlistments from the citizens of the town and from the neighboring communities of naugatuck beacon falls oxford derby and ansonia under such regulations as shall be established by the chief and assistant chiefs provided however that no person under the age of 18 years shall be a member of any company nor shall any enlistment be allowed for a term less than 12 months   1 duties of fire chief a the fire chief shall have the general superintendence of all fire apparatus belonging to the town and shall see that the same are kept in good order and repair ready for immediate use b he shall have the sole command at all fires over the assistant chiefs and other members of the fire department and over all other persons who may be present at fires c he shall direct all proper measures for the extinguishment of fires protection of property and preservation of order and he shall enforce the observance of all laws ordinances and regulations respecting fires d if at any fire he shall judge it necessary in order to extinguish the same or prevent its spread to demolish any building in town he may require and cause such building to be demolished e he shall report to the town annually giving an accurate schedule of the engines and other apparatus under his control and the state and condition of the fire department generally f he shall perform such other duties connected with the fire department as the town may from time to time require  duties of assistant chiefs it shall be the duty of the assistant chiefs to assist the chief in the discharge of his duties to receive and communicate his orders at a fire and to see that such orders are executed in the absence of the chief his duties and powers in case of a fire shall devolve upon the first assistant chief and in case of the absence of the first assistant said duties and powers shall devolve upon the next assistant chief present at such fire  powers of chief assistant chiefs the chief and assistant chief shall severally have all power and authority necessary to preserve order and enforce their commands at fires and they may use such force as may be necessary for that purpose and may command and require the aid and assistance of any person in that behalf  duties of members at fires whenever a fire shall break out in the town it shall be the duty of the officers and members of the departments to respond with their apparatus and proceed to the fire in as orderly a manner as possible upon all such occasions they shall exert themselves in the most orderly manner possible and shall obey all orders in relation thereto which the officer in command shall issue when their services at such fire are no longer required they shall return to their quarters and put their apparatus in complete order  drills and inspections the department shall be called out by the chief for the exercise and inspection of fire apparatus at such times and places as he shall appoint and when so called out shall be under the direction of the chief or in his absence one of the assistant chiefs  officers of fire companies each fire company shall consist of a captain two lieutenants a secretary a treasurer and a steward they shall be elected by the members of such company and shall hold office for one year or until they are removed and others are elected in their stead  removal of company officers members any officer or member of any company may be removed or dismissed from the fire department by the fire chief and assistant chiefs for neglect of duty disorderly conduct or disobedience to his superior officers  company records the secretary of each fire company shall keep a fair and exact roll of the members of such company with the dates of enlistment and discharge of each member and a faithful record of the election of officers and of the delinquency of members which records shall be open to inspection by the chief or his assistants at all reasonable times  bylaws of companies each company shall have power to adopt a constitution and bylaws for its regulation and government provided however that no part of the same shall be inconsistent with the provisions of this article  installation of fire hydrants the fire chief with the approbation of the fire commissioners of the town is authorized within the limit of the appropriation for that purpose each year to install fire hydrants where needed and in such places as they deem necessary without prior approval or authorization at any town meeting  volunteer fire company members and emergency medical technicians  leave from employment  exemptions a this section is enacted pursuant to public act no 89379 passed by the general assembly of the state of connecticut b the town of seymour and any person firm or corporation located within the limits of the town which employs ten or more persons at one location shall allow any active member of a volunteer fire company as defined in amendments of the connecticut general statutes or any emergency medical technician to leave his place of employment without loss of pay vacation time sick leave or earned overtime accumulation to respond to an emergency to which a volunteer fire company or emergency medical service organization of the municipality is responding c no employer shall 1 discharge discipline or reduce the wages vacation time sick leave or earned overtime accumulation of any employee because such employee is a member in a volunteer fire company or emergency medical service organization  or 2 require refusal to respond to an emergency as a condition of continued employment the requirements of this section shall not be altered by any collective bargaining agreement d any such member or technician who participates pursuant to this section shall register with the volunteer fire department or emergency medical service organization located in the town each volunteer fire company or emergency medical service organization shall maintain a list of individuals employed within the town and available to respond to an emergency between the hours of  am and  pm e the services of a member of a volunteer fire company or emergency medical service organization who leaves a place of employment to respond to an emergency shall be provided in accordance with any internal operating procedures established by the volunteer fire company or emergency medical service organization f the provisions of this section shall not apply to any employee who is the only person who is capable of operating a particular machine at a particular business such person is exempted from the provisions of this section and may not invoke its provisions g the provisions of this section shall not be applicable to any employee of the police departments of the town and such persons are exempted from the provisions of this section  reserved division 2  tax abatement footnotes  3  editors note an ordinance adopted  did not firefighters of the seymour fire department hereinafter volunteer firefighters and volunteer emergency medical service providers of the seymour ambulance association inc hereinafter volunteer ems members pursuant to connecticut general statute  1281 as amended a municipality may by ordinance provide tax relief for volunteer firefighters and ems members in an effort to attract new volunteers and retain existing volunteers such tax relief may provide either 1 an abatement of up to $100000 in property taxes due for any fiscal year or 2 an exemption applicable to the assessed value of real or personal property up to an amount equal to the quotient of $100000000 divided by the mill rate in effect at the time of assessment expressed as a whole number of dollars per $100000 of assessed value in an effort to encourage service with the seymour fire department and the seymour ambulance association inc and in recognition of the benefit that volunteer firefighters and ems members make to the public safety and well being of its residents the town of seymour has elected to make an abatement of up to $100000 in property taxes due for any fiscal year available to eligible volunteers as services as a regular active member in good standing of the seymour fire department or the seymour ambulance association inc 2  ii abatement each eligible volunteer shall be entitled to an abatement in property taxes as provided herein otherwise due from that volunteer for the fiscal year following the certification date this tax abatement is only available to volunteers who are not delinquent in entitled to any tax abatement for any program year in which the volunteer has not been credited with the requisite number of points under the point system ratified by the board of selectman the tax collector the final certified list with his approved endorsement thereon the tax collector shall then apply said abatement as follows 1 first  to any real estate taxes for real property on the town of seymour assessment list standing in the eligible volunteers name regardless of whether said property is held jointly and upon which the volunteer resides for the grand list for which the tax bill is being prepared  and 2 second  to any motor vehicle or personal property taxes for a motor vehicle or personal property on the town of seymour assessment list standing in the eligible volunteers name regardless of whether said property is held jointly for the grand list for which the tax bill is being prepared  and 3 lastly  to any other real estate taxes for real property on the town of seymour assessment list standing in the eligible volunteers name regardless of whether said property is held jointly for the grand list for which the tax bill is being prepared 4 any tax abatement earned but not fully credited in any program year may not be taken as a future credit or result in a payment to the volunteer 2  vi miscellaneous a any volunteer who regardless of reason loses his or her status as a regular active member in good standing and then regains said status may include years previously served in the seymour fire department or the seymour ambulance association
