exclusively upon stationary rails or tracks yield rightofway when required by an official sign means the act of granting the privilege of the immediate use of the intersecting roadway to traffic within the intersection and to vehicles approaching from the right or left provided that when the roadway is clear the vehicle may proceed into the intersection a1 cross reference definitions and rules of construction generally  12 obedience to police members of the police department and special police assigned to traffic duty are hereby authorized to direct all traffic in accordance with the provisions of this chapter or in emergencies as public safety or convenience may require and it shall be unlawful for any person to fail or refuse to comply with any lawful order signal or direction of a policeman it shall be unlawful for any person not authorized by law to direct or attempt to direct traffic provided that this section shall not apply to emergency accident situations where a duly authorized officer of the law is not the scene a2 signs and signals it shall be unlawful for the driver of any vehicle to disobey the instructions of any traffic sign or signal placed in view by authority of the board of police commissioners or in accordance with the laws of the state except on direction of a police officer a3 trafficcontrol signal legend a the following legend shall apply to all drivers and pedestrians when traffic at an intersection is alternately directed to proceed and to stop by the use of signals exhibiting colored lights or lighted arrows successively one at a time or in combination only the colors green red and yellow shall be used except for special pedestriancontrol signals carrying word legends these lights shall apply to drivers of vehicles and pedestrians and shall indicate the following 1 circular green alone vehicular traffic facing a green signal may proceed straight turn right or left unless a sign or marking at such place prohibits either such turn or straight except that such traffic shall yield the rightofway to pedestrians and vehicles lawfully within a crosswalk or the intersection at the time such signal was exhibited  pedestrians facing the green signal except when directed by separate pedestriancontrol signals may proceed across the highway within any marked or unmarked crosswalk 2 yellow vehicular traffic facing a steady yellow signal is thereby warned that the related green movement is being terminated or that a red indication will be exhibited immediately thereafter when vehicular traffic shall stop before entering the intersection unless so close to the intersection that a stop cannot be made in safety  pedestrians facing a steady yellow signal except when directed by separate pedestriancontrol signals are thereby advised that there is insufficient time to cross the roadway before a red indication is shown and no pedestrian shall then start to cross the roadway 3 red alone vehicular traffic facing a steady red signal alone shall stop before entering the crosswalk on the near side of the intersection or if none then before entering the intersection and remain standing until the next indication is shown  pedestrians facing a steady red signal alone except when directed by separate pedestriancontrol signals shall not enter the roadway 4 green arrow vehicular traffic facing a green arrow signal shown alone or in combination with another indication may cautiously enter the intersection only to make the movement indicated by such arrow or such other movement as is permitted by other indications shown at the same time but such vehicular traffic shall yield the rightofway to pedestrians lawfully within a crosswalk and to other traffic lawfully within the intersection 5 pedestrian signals whenever special pedestriancontrol signals exhibiting the words walk or dont walk are in place such signals shall indicate as follows a walk pedestrians facing such signals may proceed across the roadway in the direction of the signal and shall be given the rightofway by the drivers of all vehicles  b dont walk no pedestrian shall start to cross the roadway in the direction of such signal but any pedestrian who has partially completed his crossing on the walk signal shall proceed to a sidewalk or safety island while the dont walk signal is showing b when an illuminated flashing red or yellow signal is used in a traffic sign or signal it shall require obedience by vehicular traffic as follows 1 flashing red when a red lens is illuminated by rapid intermittent flashes drivers of vehicles shall stop before entering the nearest crosswalk at an intersection or at a limit line when marked or if none then before entering the intersection and the right to proceed shall be subject to the rules applicable after making a stop at a stop sign 2 flashing yellow when a yellow lens is illuminated with rapid intermittent flashes drivers of vehicles facing such signal may proceed intersection or past such signal only with caution c when lanedirectionscontrol signals are placed over the individual lanes of a street or highway vehicular traffic may travel in any lane over which a green arrow signal is shown but shall not enter or travel in any lane over which a red x signal is shown d if a trafficcontrol signal approved by the state traffic commission is erected and maintained at a place other than an intersection the provisions of this section shall be applicable except as to those provisions which by their nature can have no application any stop required shall be made at a sign or marking on the pavement indicating where the stop shall be made but in the absence of any sign or marking the stop shall be made at the signal a1 unauthorized signs no person shall place maintain or display upon or in view of any highway any unauthorized sign signal marking or device which purports to be or is an imitation of or resembles an official trafficcontrol device or railroad sign or signal or which attempts to direct the movement of traffic nor shall any person place maintain or display upon or in view of any highway any other sign which hides from view or interferes with the movement of traffic or effectiveness of any trafficcontrol device or any railroad sign or signal and no person shall place or maintain nor shall any public authority permit upon any highway any traffic or signal bearing thereon any commercial advertising any such unauthorized device is hereby declared to be a nuisance and may be removed by any policeman a1 interference with signs or signals it shall be unlawful for any person to deface injure move or interfere with any official traffic sign or signal a1 animals or bicycles every person riding a bicycle or an animal or driving any animal drawing a vehicle upon any street shall be subject to the provisions of this chapter applicable to the driver of a vehicle except those provisions which can have no application to one riding a bicycle or driving or riding an animal provided that except in business districts bicycles may be ridden on sidewalks a1 riding on running boards it shall be unlawful for any person to ride upon the fenders running boards or outside step of any vehicle except on municipal vehicles where required for municipal services a4 clinging to vehicles it shall be unlawful for any person on any street riding a bicycle motorcycle or any toy vehicle to cling to or to attach himself or his vehicle to any moving motor vehicle or wagon a4 unattended animals it shall be unlawful to leave any horse or other draft animal unattended in any street without having such animal securely fastened a4 toy vehicles it shall be unlawful for any person upon skates a coaster sled or other toy vehicle to go upon any roadway other than at a crosswalk this section shall not apply to bicycles a4 unattended vehicles no vehicle shall be left unattended while the motor of such vehicle is running  and no vehicle shall be left without a driver on any hill or incline unless the vehicle is secured against moving whenever any police officer finds a vehicle unattended upon any bridge or where such vehicle constitutes an obstruction to traffic such officer is hereby authorized to provide for the removal of such vehicle to the nearest garage or other place of safety a4 obstruction of traffic no vehicle shall be operated or allowed to remain upon the street in such a manner as to form an unreasonable obstruction to the traffic thereon a4 exemptions the provisions of this chapter regulating the movement or parking of vehicles shall not apply to the driver of any authorized emergency vehicle when responding to an emergency call but such driver upon approaching a red or stop signal or any stop sign shall slow down as necessary for safety but may proceed cautiously past such red or stop sign or signal at other times drivers of authorized emergency vehicles shall stop in obedience to a stop sign or signal no driver of any authorized emergency vehicle shall assume any special privileges under the provisions of this chapter except when such vehicle is operated in response to an emergency call or in the immediate pursuit of an actual or suspected violator of the law or except as may otherwise be provided by the general statutes a1 secs 16151630  reserved article ii  operation through streets and oneway streets a oneway streets or alleys it shall be unlawful to operate any vehicle on any street or alley designated as a oneway street or alley by regulation of the board of police commissioners in any direction other than that so designated b stop streets the driver of a vehicle shall make a complete stop in obedience to a stop sign at an intersection where a stop sign is erected at one or more entrances thereto and shall thereupon proceed cautiously yielding to the vehicles not so obliged to stop which are within the intersection or approaching so close as to constitute an immediate hazard unless traffic at such intersection is controlled by a police officer on duty in which event the directions of the police officer shall be complied with c posting signs the chief of police or any other person designated by the board of police commissioners shall post or cause to be posted suitable signs for all such oneway streets or alleys and stop intersections as have been established by the board of police commissioners acting as the traffic authority of the town provided that if such installation shall require the use of heavy equipment the board of police commissioners shall so notify the first selectman who shall cause such signs to be erected by the street department a4 u turns it shall be unlawful for the operator of any vehicle to make a u turn on any street a3 no left turn it shall be unlawful for the operator of any motor vehicle to turn left at any place when such turns are prohibited by posted sign a3 fire department vehicles  fires a upon the approach of a fire department vehicle drivers of vehicles shall comply with the provisions of his chapter relating to the approach of authorized emergency vehicles it shall be unlawful for the driver of any vehicle other than one on official business including police firemen ambulance drivers and the like to follow any fire apparatus in response to a fire alarm closer than one block or to park any vehicle within the block where fire apparatus has stopped to answer a fire alarm b it shall be further unlawful for the driver of any vehicle to drive over any unprotected hose of the fire department without the consent of the fire chief or the assistant in command a3 cross reference fire prevention and protection ch 6 speed restrictions a it shall be unlawful to drive any motor vehicle on any street not under the jurisdiction of the state in an urban district within the town at a speed in excess of 30 miles per hour or in an alley at a speed in excess of 15 miles per hour or in a school zone in excess of 20 miles per hour b the board of police commissioners shall post appropriate signs as provided in section 1631c  provided further that the speed of all vehicles having two or more solid tires shall not exceed ten miles per hour c the fact that the speed of a vehicle does not exceed the applicable maximum speed limit does not relieve the driver from the duty to decrease speed when approaching and crossing an intersection when approaching and going around a curve when approaching a hillcrest when traveling upon any narrow or winding roadway or when special hazards exist with respect to pedestrians or other traffic by reason of weather or highway conditions  and speed shall be decreased as may be necessary to avoid colliding with any person or vehicle on or entering the highway in compliance with legal requirements and the duty of all persons to use due care a4 special speed limit while passing schools no person shall drive a motor vehicle at a speed in excess of 20 miles per hour while passing a school zone school zones shall be marked by a posted sign marked school zone a4 operation of vehicles on approach of authorized emergency vehicles a upon the immediate approach of an authorized emergency vehicle when the driver is giving audible sign by siren or bell the driver of every other vehicle shall yield the rightofway and shall immediately drive to a position parallel to and as close as possible to the righthand edge or curb of the highway clear of any intersection and shall stop or remain in such position until the authorized emergency vehicle has passed except when otherwise directed by a police officer b this section shall not operate to relieve the driver of an authorized emergency vehicle from the duty to drive with due regard for the safety of all persons using the highway a4 oneway roadways and rotary traffic islands a upon a roadway designated and signposted for oneway traffic a vehicle shall be driven only in the direction designated b a vehicle passing around a rotary traffic island shall be driven only on the right of such island a4 funeral processions to be identified a funeral composed of a procession of vehicles shall be identified by having the lights of each vehicle lighted a4 drivers in a procession each driver in a funeral or other procession shall drive as near to the righthand edge of the roadway as practical and shall follow the vehicle ahead as closely as practical and safe a4 driving or other procession no driver of a vehicle shall drive between the vehicles comprising a funeral or other authorized procession while they are in motion and when such vehicles are conspicuously designated as required in section 1639 a4 secs 16421660  reserved article iii  parking stopping and the general statutes there is hereby created a parking authority which shall be known as the seymour parking authority  samemembership  terms  compensation  organization  records a the parking authority shall consist of five members appointed by the first selectman not more than three of whom shall be of the same political party those first appointed shall be designated to serve for one two three four and five years respectively  and thereafter a member shall be appointed annually to serve for five years except that any vacancy shall be filled for the unexpired portion of the term b the parking authority shall select from among its members a chairman vicechairman and secretary the members of the authority shall serve without compensation but may be reimbursed for necessary expenses c no action of the parking authority shall be valid unless authorized by a vote of the majority of its members d the parking authority shall maintain proper accounting and financial records and shall make an annual report to the first selectman  samepowers the parking authority shall have the powers mandated as obligatory by the state general statutes 1 no parking places at any time it shall be unlawful to permit any vehicle to stand in any of the following places except when necessary to avoid conflict with other traffic or in compliance with the directions of a policeman or trafficcontrol device 1 in any intersection  2 in a crosswalk  3 upon any bridge or the approach thereto  4 within 25 feet of the driveway entrance to any fire station  5 on any sidewalk  6 at any place where official signs prohibit parking  7 within 15 feet of a fire hydrant a5 alleys no person shall park a vehicle within an alley in such a manner or under such conditions as to leave available less than ten feet of the width of the roadway for the free movement of vehicular traffic an no person shall stop stand or park a vehicle within an alley in such a position as to block the driveway entrance to any abutting property a5 cab and bus stands no vehicle other than a licensed taxicab shall be parked in any area designated by posted sign as a cab stand  and no vehicle other than a bus shall be parked in a place so designated as a bus loading zone a5 time limit parking a except on sundays or holidays it shall be unlawful to park any vehicle for a longer consecutive period of time than that designated in any area designated by regulation of the board of police commissioners as a limited parking area and so marked b no vehicle shall be parked on a public highway between the hours of  midnight and  am during the months of december january february and march a5 parking motor vehicles on private property it shall be unlawful to park any motor vehicle on any private property without the consent of the owner of the property a5 vehicles for sale it shall be unlawful to park any vehicle upon any street for the purpose of displaying it for sale or to park any vehicle upon any business street from which vehicle merchandise is peddled a4 parking regulation attendants a the seymour parking authority is hereby authorized to employ up to three parking regulation attendants who shall hold office during periods of satisfactory performance and whose duties shall be as hereinafter set forth b parking regulation attendants are empowered to issue violation notices tickets on forms provided by the police department for all motor vehicle violations of vehicles parked upon business district streets or in business district parking lots in the town in violation of the general statutes the ordinances and regulations of the seymour parking authority c attendants shall serve under the direction of the chief of police who shall prescribe the hours of employment and direct the specific duties to be performed by parking regulation attendants d parking regulation attendants shall receive such compensation as shall be duly authorized by the seymour parking authority a9   14   business district parking a definitions the following words and phrases when used in this section shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this subsection business district streets for purposes of this subsection the business district streets in the town shall include the following main street broad street river street bank street from street numbers 1 north main street from bank street to main street wakeley street first street and deforest street business district parking lots the parking lot areas located on wakeley street franklin street and the leased portions of the strand theater parking lot located at the corner of north main and main streets and the parking lot on lower main street at the intersection of broad street b business district street parking it shall be unlawful to park any vehicle or to permit a vehicle to remain parked in one location on any business district street for a period longer than two hours between the hours of  am to  pm monday inclusive except as may be otherwise posted in designated areas approved by the seymour parking authority this restriction shall not apply to sundays and the legal observances of the following holidays new years day memorial day independence day labor day thanksgiving day and christmas day any vehicle parked for a period of longer than two hours on a business district street may be fined successively at intervals not less than two hours apart c business district parking in parking lots 1 it shall be unlawful to park any vehicle or to permit a vehicle to remain parked in any business district parking lot between the hours of  am and  am monday inclusive without displaying an approved parking permit sticker for the particular parking lot wherein the vehicle is parked issued to the owner or driver of the vehicle by the seymour parking authority the parking permit sticker shall be affixed on the inside of the vehicles front windshield at the bottom corner of the passenger side in such a manner that a parking attendant or police officer may easily view the sticker at a distance when standing in back of the vehicle 2 an application for a parking permit shall be made at the police department if an application is approve a parking permit sticker will be issued to the applicant applications will be approved or denied by the seymour parking authority or by whomever the seymour parking authority may designate to do so priority for such permits will be given to the owners and employees of businesses located in the business district and residents living within the business district 3 an annual fee shall be charged by the seymour parking authority for the issuance or renewal of a parking permit all parking permits shall expire and are subject to renewal on june thirtieth of each year the fee shall be $1000 if any parking permit is issued between december 31st and june 30th the parking permit fee shall be $500 for the period from the time of issuance thirtieth 4 a parking permit sticker shall display a parking permit number and may be used only on the vehicle for which it was issued a maximum of two parking permit stickers for two motor vehicles may be issued to each applicant however the individual to whom a permit has been issued may be issued a replacement sticker for another vehicle without paying an additional fee if the previously issued sticker is surrendered in order to transfer the permit to another vehicle owned or driven by the applicant upon completing the appropriate form or forms at the police department if the previously issued parking permit sticker is not surrendered a fee for a new parking permit sticker will be charged 5 parking permit stickers are not transferable and cannot be used on any vehicle other than the vehicle for which the permit was issued 6 the seymour parking authority or whomever they designate to approve or deny applications for parking permits may issue parking permit stickers to applicants with specific restrictions 7 a courtesy or temporary parking permit sticker may be issued at the discretion of the seymour parking authority or its designee until such time as an application for a parking permit is granted or denied 8 any vehicle not displaying the required parking permit sticker during the hours of  am am monday inclusive shall be subject to a fine andor may be towed at the owners expense 9 all vehicles parked in the business district parking lots shall be parked in the spaces provided between the designated parking lines any vehicle not so parked shall be subject to a fine andor may be towed at the owners expense 10 in the event that the status of a parking permit holder changes so that he or she no longer qualifies for a parking permit his or her parking permit and sticker shall be revoked immediately without any necessary action by the seymour parking authority or other administrator of this parking program there will be no rebate of the parking permit fee if the permit is revoked 11 any person who transfers a parking permit sticker to an unauthorized vehicle shall be fined in accordance with section 19 and such person may have his parking permit revoked the unauthorized vehicle may also be towed at the owners expense  13   handicapped parking a applicability this section shall apply to all new and existing sites that have a parking area for 25 or more vehicles including but not limited to shopping centers office buildings commercial buildings mercantile buildings factories warehouses storage buildings convalescent homes apartment buildings and schools but excluding public parking areas controlled by the local traffic authority in addition the local traffic authority may designate handicapped parking spaces on town roads which shall be of such size and location as they may specify b use of specially designated spaces after establishment of specially marked parking spaces for handicapped persons no persons shall park a motor vehicle in such space unless a handicapped person is either a passenger or operator of the vehicle and the vehicle contains a designation issued by the commissioners of motor vehicles pursuant to the general statutes which designation shall be visible as per the general statutes or a handicapped designation issued by another state parking spaces for the handicapped shall be located as close as possible to elevators ramps walkways and entrances and to curb cuts and other structures permitting sidewalk access to a handicapped person the exact location and number of spaces shall be designated by the traffic authority or his designee but in no event may the traffic authority designate fewer spaces than required by state law c suggested number of spaces to be provided on each site having parking spaces for at least 25 vehicles the parking authority may require that one space shall be specially designated and reserved for handicapped parking additional spaces for handicapped parking may be required by the traffic authority in accordance with the following table total parking on site number of handicapped parking spaces 2550 1 51100 2 101150 3 151200 4 201300 5 301400 6 401500 7 5011000 2% of total over 1000 20 plus 1 for each 100 over 1000 d marking of spaces each such space designated for handicapped parking shall be not less than 15 feet in width including three feet of cross hatch unless the same would create a nonconforming condition in which event the existing parking stall width shall be permitted each space shall be designated by above grade signs with white lettering against a blue background and shall bear the words handicapped parking state permit required such signs on markings shall be erected installed and maintained by and at the expense of the owner operator lessee or tenant of said site and shall further indicate that unauthorized use of said space shall subject the violator to a fine if the signs and markings called for in this section are not installed within 30 days after written request by the town traffic authority the town may proceed to install the same and impose the costs thereof against the owner of the site e penalty whenever any vehicle shall be found parked in violation of this section any police officer or parking attendant may issue a citation for such violation which citation shall provide for a fine in the amount as stated on said citation and said fine shall be payable to the police department within 48 hours after issuance f owners responsibility for violations the registered owner of any vehicle parked in violation of this section shall be presumed to be the operator at the time of the violation    state law reference parking privileges of handicapped persons generally gs  14253a  parking privileges of handicapped veterans gs  14254 tickets for offenses against the provisions of this article the police officers or parking regulation attendants after making note of the registration number of the vehicle and the name of the offender where possible may issue a traffic violation ticket on a form approved by the chief of police notifying the offender to appear at the police station such officer or parking regulation attendant may sign a complaint for the issuance of a warrant if the offender does not appear as the time and place so specified    prima facie proof the fact that an automobile which is illegally parked is registered in the name of a person shall be considered prima facie proof that such person was in control of the automobile at the time of such parking a7   parking violations a any person accused of a violation of the provisions of this article or any regulation of the seymour parking authority prohibiting parking a vehicle in a designated area or restricting the length of time a vehicle may be parked there may settle and compromise the claim against him or her for such illegal parking by paying to the town the sum as prescribed on the violation ticket within the allotted time as directed on the violation ticket if said fine is not paid within the allotted time said fine shall double in amount every 48 hours until it reaches the amount of $5000 at which time a warrant shall be applied for b the board of police commissioners may recommend from time to time to the board of selectmen modifications of parking fines the board of selectmen shall be responsible for determining the amount of parking violation fines c the members of the police department as well as parking regulation attendants are hereby directed to refrain from instituting a prosecution for the alleged offense if the payment pursuant to this subsection has been made within 120 hours of the time of this issuance of the ticket    towing cars away a the police department and all members thereof assigned to traffic duty are hereby authorized to remove and tow away or have removed and towed away by commercial towing service any car or other vehicle illegally parked in any place where such parked vehicle creates or constitutes a traffic hazard blocks the use of a fire hydrant or obstructs or may obstruct the movement of any emergency vehicle or obstructs removal of snow between the first day of december and the ensuing march 31st b cars towed away for illegal parking shall be stored in a safe place and shall be restored to the owner or operator of such car upon payment of the parking violation at the police department within 48 hours after the time such car was removed plus costs of towing and storage a7   state law reference removal of abandoned motor vehicles by municipalities gs  14150a pending criminal prosecutions nothing within the provisions of this article shall be deemed to affect the disposition or prosecution of any criminal prosecution pending at the time of the enactment of this ordinances a8 utilities footnotes  1  charter reference board of public works  1013  water pollution control authority  1014 cross reference health and sanitation ch power of town to regulate the laying etc of water pipes drains sewers etc in the streets and public places gs  7148c6biii  power of town to regulate and prohibit the construction etc of sinks cesspools gs  7148c7c  municipal waterworks systems gs  7234 et seq  municipal sewerage systems gs  7245 et seq  sewer districts gs  7324 et seq  water resources gs  251 et seq  sewer revenue bonds gs  72597266 article i  in general secs 1711725  reserved article ii  sewers division 1  generally pipe depth no earthenware pipe shall be laid less than two and onehalf feet deep underground pipe laid at less than such depth shall be of heavy cast iron with well caulked and leaded joints  standards for pipes and joints a inverts all pipes shall be laid with ends abutting and true to line and grade so that they will form a sewer with a smooth and uniform invert b support the pipes shall be so laid as to be evenly supported throughout the length of the barrel with no weight resting on the bell c joints joints shall be thoroughly and carefully caulked with a closely twisted hemp or jute gasket untarred in one continuous piece of sufficient thickness to hold the pipes in the required relative positions and in such way as to make the gaskets substantially watertight the plastic compound to be used in jointing the pipe shall be steam reduced asphalt with a melting point of between 165 degrees fahrenheit to 185 degrees fahrenheit and acid filler 100 percent of which will pass a 280 mesh sieve the compound shall be heated in a gasoline or other suitable furnace to a temperature slightly above that at which it will pour rapidly and smoothly at which it shall be kept until it is used after the jute gasket has been caulked a pipe jointed or joint runner shall be placed round the pipe in a manner similar to that used in pouring lead joints except that the opening shall be offset from the center at the top of the pipe in such a manner that the jointing compound will flow down only one side of the pipe the melted compound shall be poured into the joint until the liquid rises on the side of the pipe opposite to that in which it was poured and the joint is completely filled enough compound shall be contained in the ladle or pouring bucket to pour one joint complete without interrupting the pouring if a joint shall be found to be imperfectly filled the joint compound shall be melted out or cut out and the joint repoured d stopping unconnected ends the ends of all pipes not to be immediately connected with must be securely stopped with vitrified stoneware covers with plastic joints e covering the pipes shall be covered with fine soil dry and free from stone or lumps carefully and thoroughly tamped around and over them to a depth of at least one foot f ditch drainage during work the ditch must at all times be kept dry during the pipe laying g preventing of sand or dirt the greatest care must be taken to prevent the entrance of sand or dirt into the house sewer or public sewer  backfilling a backfilling must be solidly tamped in horizontal layers not over six inches thick or puddled by flooding the trench and allowing the filling material to settle water the backfilling must be done immediately after the completion and inspection of that part of the sewer lying in the public highway and done so as to make the sidewalk curb gutter and highway in as good condition as they were previous to the commencement of the work and to the satisfaction of the authorities having jurisdiction thereof b the backfilling of the trench in the highway shall be thoroughly tamped and maintained until a permanent patch shall be placed after settlement has taken place and when in the opinion of the inspector no future settlement is anticipated the trench shall be excavated to a depth of eight inches below the surface of the pavement and repaired with at least six inches of bank run gravel and not less than two inches of bituminous material which shall be rolled or tamped to conform to the crosssection of the pavement the materials method of placing and final result shall be subject to the approval of the inspector failure of the patch shall not relieve the owner or contractor of responsibility in this matter and upon failure the work found defective shall be replaced upon order of the sewer inspector  removal of rock in sewer trenches all rock shall be removed at least 15 feet in advance of the laying of the sewer connection and six inches outside the outside lines of the barrel of the pipe after the removal of the rock the trench shall be filled with sand or fine gravel and thoroughly rammed  replacement of unsuitable material in trench wherever in the opinion of the board of selectmen or its authorized agent the bottom of the trench is of material unsuitable for a foundation it shall be removed and replaced with dry material plank concrete sand cushion or concrete cradle as directed  safety precautions to protect public any opening made or any dirt pile material or equipment in or on the public highway must have sufficient barricades and red lights at night and all other necessary precautions to guard the public effectually against all accidents from the beginning to the end of the work  precautions when blasting in case blasting is done the trench shall be carefully covered and all property fully protected from damage care must be taken to guard the public sewers and all underground pipes or mains from damage from concussion and flying fragments the owner or contractor to whom the permit is issued shall pay all costs of any repairs to such sewers pipes and mains made necessary by the operation also any damage to person or property occasioned by the use of explosives by a contractor shall be assumed and paid by the contractor to the person injured  connections with town sewers a required for dwellings every dwelling or tenanted building hereafter erected in the town shall be connected with the town sewer before occupancy if such connection is possible at a reasonable expense b minimum grade no house sewer connection with the public sewer shall be laid with a grade of less than one inch fall in four feet without a written permit signed by the sewer authority or its authorized agent specifying the minimum grade that will be permitted c requirements specifications every house sewer hereafter laid connecting with the public sewer from a point two feet outside of the outside face of the foundation walls except as hereinafter provided shall be best quality vitrified salt glazed tile of good shape sound with a clear ring when struck with a hammer and having only very small cracks capable of being covered in the joints when laid  or of cast iron pipe extra heavy at least as large as five inches in diameter weighing not less than 17 pounds per foot in lengths not less than four feet laid with leaded joints all sixinch tile pipe shall have deep and wide sockets and shall conform to the standard specifications of the american society for testing materials d traps obstructions in connecting any house drainage system with the town sewer no trap or any kind of obstruction to the free flow of air whole course of the soil pipe shall be allowed but the house drainage system shall be separated from the main line of the pipe by a water trap therein e approval supervision no house drain shall be connected with any town sewer pipe until the sewer inspector shall have given his consent thereto and every such connection shall be made under the immediate supervision of said inspector f connections serving several buildings each building in the area served by a public sewer must be connected separately and independently with the sewer house connection branch opposite the building or nearest in the downstream direction groupings of buildings on one house sewer will not be permitted save by special act of the sewer authority and for good sanitary reasons g pipe diameter between sewer and soil pipe all pipes from the connection with the town sewer to the soil pipe shall be at least five inches in interior diameter h connection to rain surface sump pump discharge rain water leaders and surface water or sump pump discharge pipes shall not be connected to the town sewer i connection to steam exhaust no exhaust from any steam engine or blowoff from any steam boiler shall be connected directly with any sewer or drain connecting with the public sewer but all such steam shall be condensed before passing into the sewer   oxh5  secs of inspector a before proceeding to construct any portion of the drainage system of any building in the town the person doing the work shall make written application to the sewer inspector describing the work contemplated where located and when the same is to be commenced b this description of the work shall be made to the satisfaction of the sewer inspector and shall be accompanied by a permit fee as established by the sewer authority c the sewer inspector upon approving of the same shall give a written permit for such work and no work shall be commenced before such permit is received d the sewer inspector shall keep a record of all permits granted and fees received by himself and shall make an annual report showing the same in the same manner and at the same time as is provided for other town officials  indemnity insurance to protect town required any person applying for a permit under the provisions of this division shall file a certificate of insurance indemnifying the town consequence of or resulting from any work performed by said applicant his agents or employees or from any improper materials used in the work or from any negligence in guarding such work or from any june first immediately following the excavation by a permanent pavement to be approved by the board of selectmen  approval of materials workmanship by inspector all materials used in sewer placed and finished to his acceptance  secs 17551765  reserved division 3  sewer authority footnotes  3  charter reference water pollution control authority  1014 established  appointment of members there is hereby established a board to be called the sewer authority consisting of nine members who shall be electors of the town the members of the sewer authority shall be appointed by the first selectman for a threeyear term in accordance with the provisions of the town charter a   terms in the initial appointment of the sewer authority commencing on  two members shall be appointed for a term of one year two members for a term of two years and two members for a term of three years thereafter such appointments shall be for a period of three years upon appointment effective  three additional members shall be appointed increasing the sewer authority from six to nine members upon such appointment one member shall be appointed for a term of one year  one member for a term of two years  and one for a term of three years thereafter such appointments shall be for a period of three years a1   officers the sewer authority shall elect from among its members a chairman a vicechairman a secretary and a treasurer and in the absence of any such officers except the chairman the authority may elect other members to temporarily serve replacement appointments shall be made by the first selectman for the remaining term of the original appointment a2 compensation there shall be no compensation allowed for any member of the sewer authority except as provided under section 42 of the town charter a3 removal the members of the sewer authority may be removed for 1 failure to properly and expeditiously levy sewer assessments for projects duly authorized by the town and constructed by the authority  2 failure to obtain proper and valid easements for sewer rightsofway and have them duly filed on the land records of the town  3 failure to adhere to the towns bidding ordinance requirements for goods and services allocated within their budget  4 failure to live within their budget as approved by the towns fiscal process  5 failure to properly account for the income funds earned by the sewer authority  6 failure to obtain planning and zoning approval for any new sewer projects  7 failure to apply for or properly follow up applications for federal or state subsidies for sewer projects the removal shall become effective only after a hearing called for that purpose and supported by a majority vote of the board of selectmen a4 powers and duties the sewer authority shall be empowered to provide for the planning construction maintenance and operation of a sanitary sewerage system for the town as provided by the general statutes the sewer authority may establish and revise rules and regulations for the supervision management control operation and use of a sewerage system including rules and regulations prohibiting or regulating the discharge into a sewerage system of any sewage or any stormwater runoff which in the opinion of the sewer authority will adversely affect any part of any process of the sewerage system the rules and regulations shall become effective only after a duly called hearing and shall be available to the public in booklet form b members prohibited from being employees no member of the sewer authority shall also be an employee of the sewer authority a5 secs 17731785  reserved division 4  sewer inspector footnotes  4  cross reference appointment there shall be a sewer inspector and an assistant in the town who shall
